.main-inner .fauxcolumn-right-outer {
width: 350px;
}
.main-inner .column-left-outer {
width: 0;
right: 100%;
margin-left: -0;
}
.main-inner .column-right-outer {
width: 350px;
margin-right: -350px;
}

                                        &lt;div class="date-outer"&gt;
                                      
&lt;h2 class='date-header'&gt;
&lt;span&gt;
Thursday, 12 February 2015
&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;/h2&gt;

                                        &lt;div class="date-posts"&gt;
                                      
&lt;div class='post-outer'&gt;
&lt;div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'&gt;
&lt;meta content='http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Y-6yRbmitQo/U6eRKaIxBCI/AAAAAAAABh4/zz1w4TcR9AM/s1600/Goals.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/&gt;
&lt;meta content='2480335764212217316' itemprop='blogId'/&gt;
&lt;meta content='6795020499654530520' itemprop='postId'/&gt;
&lt;a name='6795020499654530520'&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
&lt;a href='http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2015/02/how-to-cope-with-being-on-psychiatric.html'&gt;
How to cope with being on psychiatric medication and get your life together
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6795020499654530520' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-RW-UHwVMPfk/VNy9Dmfz-dI/AAAAAAAAB_o/dSTkH01pVzM/s1600/images.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Most&nbsp;psychiatric medication is designed to keep you on a even keel. Usually your mood is like a wave, it fluctuates between high. low and every place in-between. Most&nbsp;psychiatric medication is designed to remove the extreme highs and lows and keep you stable. This means that probably won't feel as down or as good as you used too. You mood will be stuck in a bizarre middle zone where you won't be as excited or upset about things and you might feel a little bit "off". Usually&nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;psychiatric&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&nbsp;medication is the lesser of two evils.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Having a something to help provide a stable mood is only one part of the battle. Psychiatric&nbsp;medication is not going to be the answer, rather a means to help you learn the skills and acquire the habits that will put you in good stead for the rest of your life.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;First of all make sure you are on the right dosage or type of drug. To do this make sure to have honest communicate with your&nbsp;psychiatrist about your symptons and learn about the side effects. As mentioned earlier, Taking&nbsp;psychiatric medication probably will not make you feel 100% nor will it cure all your problems so try not to jump from drug to drug or doctor shop until you have found the "perfect solution". There will never be the exactly perfect conditions to start working on yourself so try to work with the stability that the drugs provide&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;If you read the horror stories on the internet or read a hand out pertaining to your medication. Chance are that you have heard about withdrawals. Withdrawals happen when your body has adapted to the presence of medication. When you take the medication away, your body might go haywire as all the systems try to compensate for the lack of medication. Withdrawals can be worse than your illness/s and can even mimic it. Even if you are not on the right medication or feel great, you could still have withdrawal effects. So try not to play doctor and attempt to come of your medication by yourself and if you do, try to taper off slowly. Roughly only about a 6th of people manage to get off some of the more potent medications going cold turkey.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Once you are stable and used to medication its time to start working on your problems. The best way to do this is to get into the right shape to tackle them. This involves doing the basic fundamentals of life well&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Nutrition&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Hydration&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Exercise&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Sleep&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Mindfulness&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Support&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;b&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Nutrition&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Food is comprise of various chemicals, and like all chemicals have differing effects on the body.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Try to eat a healthy balance diet of 5-6 meals a day spaced 2-3 hours apart. This will help regulated your mood which is important to help supplement the effects of your medication&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;b&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Hydration&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;It is important to drink an adequate amount of water. Staying hydrated is absolutely a fundamental part of your keeping your mood steady. So many process in the body rely on being hydrated. Try to aim for 2-3 liters of water a day excluding the amount of water you get from food.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;b&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Exercise&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Staying active is an important part of keeping your mood from fluctuating to much. Good exercise will help improve your mood and give you something positive to work towards and will serve as distraction/outlet&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;b&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Sleep&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Sleep is absolute essential to well being and mental health. Try to aim to go to bed and wake up at the same time each day to get into a good circadian rhythm. If you can't get to sleep, try to avoid taking sleeping pills and try eating/drinking something rich in tryptophan such as milk, cheese or turky to help you sleep instead. Alternatively you could ask your doctor for melatonin which is one of the only sleeping pills that won't mess you up.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;b&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Mindfulness&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Being aware and staying on top of your emotions is vital to mental health. Mindfulness is a very good tool for this. Check out my other posts on mindfulness &lt;a href="http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/06/mindfullness-101.html" target="_blank"&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; and h&lt;a href="http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/06/mindfulness-102-how-to-be-mindful.html" target="_blank"&gt;ere&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;b&gt;Support&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
No man is an island so it is important to reach out to receive and &lt;u&gt;give&lt;/u&gt;&nbsp;support. Discuss friends, family and mental health team ways that they can support you and you can help them. It is important to reciprocate the support as life is a team sport. It will help boost your confidence and self esteem.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;
&lt;b style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;The next stage... Goals&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;While &nbsp;you are getting the basics down to a fine art, remember that getting the fundamentals right is a constant challenge for everyone. Once you got to point where you are reasonably comfortable with doing the basics it time to move onto the next stage, setting and carrying out goals.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="color: #222222;"&gt;&lt;span style="line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;Having and carrying out goals and planning your life are key step into your recovery and getting your life together. Goals are a way to&nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;systematically&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="color: #222222;"&gt;&lt;span style="line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;&nbsp;work towards improving your life in the most effective way.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&nbsp;This is the stage where you get to recreate your life and take control!&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;div class="bq_s" style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;
&lt;div class="bq_fq bq_fq_lrg" style="margin: 0px;"&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;A man without a goal is like a ship without a rudder. - Thomas Carlyle&nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;div class="bq_fq_a"&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;Its is important to have goals that are reasonable. Having clear goals that are realistic, challenging and energizing will lead to more positive outcomes than goals that are too easy or unrealistic.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;The probability of successfully completing a goal is related to how difficult the goal is&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="background-color: white; clear: both; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Y-6yRbmitQo/U6eRKaIxBCI/AAAAAAAABh4/zz1w4TcR9AM/s1600/Goals.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; color: #888888; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em; text-decoration: none;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Y-6yRbmitQo/U6eRKaIxBCI/AAAAAAAABh4/zz1w4TcR9AM/s1600/Goals.jpg" style="-webkit-box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0980392) 1px 1px 5px; background-attachment: initial; background-clip: initial; background-image: initial; background-origin: initial; background-position: initial; background-repeat: initial; background-size: initial; border: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.0980392) 1px 1px 5px; padding: 5px; position: relative;" /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;The highest level of effort occurs when the task is moderately difficult&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;The lowest levels of effort occur when the task is very easy or very hard&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;&nbsp;Goals that are specific and difficult consistently led to higher performance than just urging people to do their best.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white;"&gt;&lt;span style="color: #222222;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;span style="line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;By focusing on one goal at a time, People are more likely to be able to improve a wide variety of&nbsp; skills and abilities and actually&nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;achieve&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;span style="line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;&nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="color: #222222;"&gt;&lt;span style="line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;their&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="color: #222222; font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;span style="line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;&nbsp;goals&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;Having a list of short term goals to work on each day is a very effective way to reach our hopes and dreams&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;There are five steps taking control of your life using goals&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;b style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;1. Choose your big long term goals&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;A good way to set goals is to choose a goal from each aspect of&nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href="http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/06/improving-wellness.html" style="background-color: white; color: #888888; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px; text-decoration: none;" target="_blank"&gt;wellness&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;&nbsp; These are perfect examples of big long term goals. These are long term that are challenging and pursing them will improve your life&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;b style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;2. Break down big goals&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;Make goals more obtainable by breaking them down into smaller manageable, concrete activities. These are goals you can complete in a day or less&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;b style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;3. Make a plan&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;Decide how and when you will do the sub goals. Try and include you friends and family in your sub goals&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;b style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;4. Carry out your plan&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;Spend time each day working on your sub goals and eventually you will obtain your big goal&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;b style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;5. Be flexible&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: inherit; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;Update your plan as you encounter new challenges or if you get bored and want to try something new&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;
&lt;ol style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;&lt;/ol&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;For the process to work well, you have to want to do all the goals on your list and they have to be realistic. Focus on sub goals that you find enjoyable or you believe will help you with your bigger goals.&nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;There are five major benefits to pursing goals this way&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;1. Confidence&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;2. Meaning and purpose&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;3. Social connection&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;4. Commitment&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;" /&gt;&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; line-height: 18.4799995422363px;"&gt;5. Flexibility&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style='clear: both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;

&lt;h2 class='date-header'&gt;
&lt;span&gt;
Monday, 10 November 2014
&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;/h2&gt;

                                        &lt;div class="date-posts"&gt;
                                      
&lt;div class='post-outer'&gt;
&lt;div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'&gt;
&lt;meta content='2480335764212217316' itemprop='blogId'/&gt;
&lt;meta content='5345979003266512345' itemprop='postId'/&gt;
&lt;a name='5345979003266512345'&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
&lt;a href='http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/11/rory-sutherland-perspective-is.html'&gt;
Rory Sutherland: Perspective is everything
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-5345979003266512345' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;object class="BLOGGER-youtube-video" classid="clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000" codebase="http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0" data-thumbnail-src="https://ytimg.googleusercontent.com/vi/iueVZJVEmEs/0.jpg" height="266" width="320"&gt;&lt;param name="movie" value="https://youtube.googleapis.com/v/iueVZJVEmEs&amp;source=uds" /&gt;&lt;param name="bgcolor" value="#FFFFFF" /&gt;&lt;param name="allowFullScreen" value="true" /&gt;&lt;embed width="320" height="266"  src="https://youtube.googleapis.com/v/iueVZJVEmEs&amp;source=uds" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" allowfullscreen="true"&gt;&lt;/embed&gt;&lt;/object&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px; line-height: 17px;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px; line-height: 17px;"&gt;The circumstances of our lives may matter less than how we see them, says Rory Sutherland. At TEDxAthens, he makes a compelling case for how reframing is the key to happiness.&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;div style='clear: both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-footer'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-footer-line post-footer-line-1'&gt;
&lt;span class='post-author vcard'&gt;

&lt;div class='post-outer'&gt;
&lt;div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'&gt;
&lt;meta content='2480335764212217316' itemprop='blogId'/&gt;

&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
&lt;a href='http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/11/kelly-mcgonigal-how-to-make-stress-your.html'&gt;
Kelly McGonigal: How to make stress your friend
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4628636009928347923' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;object class="BLOGGER-youtube-video" classid="clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000" codebase="http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0" data-thumbnail-src="https://ytimg.googleusercontent.com/vi/RcGyVTAoXEU/0.jpg" height="266" width="320"&gt;&lt;param name="movie" value="https://youtube.googleapis.com/v/RcGyVTAoXEU&amp;source=uds" /&gt;&lt;param name="bgcolor" value="#FFFFFF" /&gt;&lt;param name="allowFullScreen" value="true" /&gt;&lt;embed width="320" height="266"  src="https://youtube.googleapis.com/v/RcGyVTAoXEU&amp;source=uds" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" allowfullscreen="true"&gt;&lt;/embed&gt;&lt;/object&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: arial, sans-serif; line-height: 17px;"&gt;Stress. It makes your heart pound, your breathing quicken and your forehead sweat. But while stress has been made into a public health enemy, new research suggests that stress may only be bad for you if you believe that to be the case. Psychologist Kelly McGonigal urges us to see stress as a positive, and introduces us to an unsung mechanism for stress reduction: reaching out to others.&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;div style='clear: both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;

&lt;h2 class='date-header'&gt;
&lt;span&gt;
Saturday, 8 November 2014
&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;/h2&gt;

                                        &lt;div class="date-posts"&gt;
                                      
&lt;div class='post-outer'&gt;
&lt;div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'&gt;
&lt;meta content='2480335764212217316' itemprop='blogId'/&gt;
&lt;meta content='6287051721723515257' itemprop='postId'/&gt;
&lt;a name='6287051721723515257'&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
&lt;a href='http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/06/mindfulness-102-how-to-be-mindful.html'&gt;
Mindfulness 102 - How to be mindful throughout the day
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6287051721723515257' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
&lt;b&gt;Why be mindful?&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
There are a whole host of positive benefits of practicing mindful meditation.&nbsp; Below is a list of some of the benefits of mindfulness meditation&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Being more effective&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Experience less suffering&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Get more out of each moment&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Being more in touch with oneself&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Better emotional regulation&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Reliving stress&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Improving sleep&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Lower blood pressure&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Improving mental health&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Facilitates meta cognition&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
When people think of mindfulness they usually think of people meditating cross legged and focusing on their. However mindfulness can be used in a far more active capacity throughout the day. Someone can be mindful of anything in the present moment, including thoughts, sensations, emotions, surroundings and activites&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Mindfulness mediation trains someone to continually refocus their attention on the present moment while exploring sensations with an open curious mind. Mindfulness increase the quality and duration of conscious attention by allowing someone to focus on one thing and if their mind wanders to experience the distraction and then gently refocus on the current activity.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Single tasking is a core aspect of mindfulness as being mindful allows someone to fully experience one thing. &lt;a href="http://www.tandfonline.com/doi/abs/10.1080/17470210903249365" target="_blank"&gt;Studies&lt;/a&gt; have shown the single tasking mindfully is more effective than multitasking.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
The following are ways to be mindful throughout the day&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt;Practice mindfulness during routine activties&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Some people have done their routine so many times that it becomes a habit and they do it automatically without paying any conscious attention to what they are doing. Routine activities are an excellent opportunity to practice being mindful &lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt;Eat with mindfulness&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
If you wolf down your food then you miss out on the chance to savor the experience. Next time you sit down to a meal try to eat each bite mindfully and maybe even play with your food mindfully&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt;Focus on the body&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Being mindful of sensations in your body is as easy as doing a body scan and paying attention to each body part. This allows greater connection with your body&lt;b&gt; &lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt;Pay attention to breathing&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
If nothing in the moment seems interesting then returning to being mindful of breathing is always a good idea&lt;b&gt;. &lt;/b&gt;Whenever you become aware of your own breathing (like now) try and see how long you can maintain that awareness&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt;Meditate upon waking up and going to bed&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Waking up and meditating is a great way to set up your day and meditating at night is good for getting to sleep and dealing with insomnia&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt;Work with mindfulness&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Throw yourself into your work and when you notice your mind wandering then gently redirect it to your current project then be astounded much you get done&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt; &lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt; &lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt;&nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;a href="http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/06/mindfullness-101.html" target="_blank"&gt;Mindfulness 101&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;div style='clear: both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;

&lt;div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'&gt;
&lt;meta content='2480335764212217316' itemprop='blogId'/&gt;
&lt;meta content='7191804152021887467' itemprop='postId'/&gt;
&lt;a name='7191804152021887467'&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
&lt;a href='http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/06/mindfullness-101.html'&gt;
Mindfulness 101
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7191804152021887467' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Mindfulness is the ability to&lt;b&gt; &lt;/b&gt;be aware moment by moment of thoughts, feelings, body sensations and the surrounding environment. Mindfulness is important to fully live in the present moment and experience life. The practice of mindfulness improves intellectual, emotional, physical and spiritual wellness through being more connected to the present moment.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Mindfulness becomes easier with practice, the more mindfulness is practiced the more automatic mindfulness becomes.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
The following are two basic exercises, focusing on breathing, to help incorporate mindfulness into daily life&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt;Meditation&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Meditation brings many benefits. All is required is to retire to a quiet place and get comfortable. The traditional cross legged position is a great way to start but in reality you sit, lie down, stand, or adopt any pose that feels comfortable. Once settled, focus on your breathing. Once attention is noticed having moved away from breathing, simple refocus it on&nbsp; breathing&lt;b&gt;&lt;/b&gt;. Continue this for at least five minuets and go on as long as you feel comfortable&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Alternatively listen to guided meditations, an example is &lt;a href="http://marc.ucla.edu/body.cfm?id=22" target="_blank"&gt;this website&lt;/a&gt;. Plenty of more mindfulness meditation are found online&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt;Breathing&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Still focusing on breath, mindfulness can be as simple as focusing and refocusing on breathing during daily activities. The more this is done the easier it becomes and the greater the quality of attention becomes.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Check out Mindfulness 102 &lt;a href="http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/06/mindfulness-102-how-to-be-mindful.html" target="_blank"&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
&lt;a href='http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/11/voracious-vocabulary.html'&gt;
Voracious Vocabulary
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8825943336562684506' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
Having a well developed vocabulary is one of the main keys to understanding new concepts and ideas and learning new words is a great way to expand your intellect. Having a robust vocabulary assists you in becoming fluent in areas like politics, geography, military, science and the humanities.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;a href="http://www.vocabulary.com/" target="_blank"&gt;Vocabulary.com &lt;/a&gt;helps bring you next level mastery of vocabulary. Further bolstering your ability to communicate and express your self with ease while providing a rewarding and satisfying challenge.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
In no time you will be an excogitator who deliberates&nbsp;prudently upon his discourse.
&lt;div style='clear: both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;

Yes, I survived cancer. But that doesn't define me
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-1585358064228191780' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue Custom', 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 33px;"&gt;Debra Jarvis had worked as a hospital chaplain for nearly 30 years when she was diagnosed with cancer. And she learned quite a bit as a patient. In a witty, daring talk, she explains how the identity of &#8220;cancer survivor&#8221; can feel static. She asks us all to claim our hardest experiences, while giving ourselves room to grow and evolve.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue Custom', 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 33px;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;object width="320" height="266" class="BLOGGER-youtube-video" classid="clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000" codebase="http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0" data-thumbnail-src="https://ytimg.googleusercontent.com/vi/4n8qT0vQbWk/0.jpg"&gt;&lt;param name="movie" value="https://youtube.googleapis.com/v/4n8qT0vQbWk&amp;source=uds" /&gt;&lt;param name="bgcolor" value="#FFFFFF" /&gt;&lt;param name="allowFullScreen" value="true" /&gt;&lt;embed width="320" height="266"  src="https://youtube.googleapis.com/v/4n8qT0vQbWk&amp;source=uds" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" allowfullscreen="true"&gt;&lt;/embed&gt;&lt;/object&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue Custom', 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 33px;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue Custom', 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; line-height: 33px;"&gt;It is important to remember when you are suffering from a illness or a trauma that your suffering is not what you are. You are not your illness&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;div style='clear: both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;

&lt;div class='post-outer'&gt;
&lt;div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'&gt;
&lt;meta content='2480335764212217316' itemprop='blogId'/&gt;

&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
&lt;a href='http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/09/7-rules-for-making-more-happiness.html'&gt;
7 Rules for Making More Happiness
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6882852121251974292' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;object width="320" height="266" class="BLOGGER-youtube-video" classid="clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000" codebase="http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0" data-thumbnail-src="https://ytimg.googleusercontent.com/vi/eMVWSUeeg8A/0.jpg"&gt;&lt;param name="movie" value="https://youtube.googleapis.com/v/eMVWSUeeg8A&amp;source=uds" /&gt;&lt;param name="bgcolor" value="#FFFFFF" /&gt;&lt;param name="allowFullScreen" value="true" /&gt;&lt;embed width="320" height="266"  src="https://youtube.googleapis.com/v/eMVWSUeeg8A&amp;source=uds" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" allowfullscreen="true"&gt;&lt;/embed&gt;&lt;/object&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px; line-height: 17px;"&gt;Using simple, delightful illustrations, designer Stefan Sagmeister shares his latest thinking on happiness -- both the conscious and unconscious kind. His seven rules for life and design happiness can (with some customizations) apply to everyone seeking more joy.&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;div style='clear: both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-footer'&gt;

&lt;meta content='2480335764212217316' itemprop='blogId'/&gt;
&lt;meta content='4816731519235528392' itemprop='postId'/&gt;
&lt;a name='4816731519235528392'&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
&lt;a href='http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/09/the-secrets-of-happiness.html'&gt;
The Secrets of Happiness
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4816731519235528392' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
&lt;header style="background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #111111; font-family: Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 22px;"&gt;&lt;h1 style="background: transparent; border: 0px; font-size: 30px; font-weight: normal; line-height: 40px; margin: 0px 0px 15px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;"&gt;
&lt;a href="http://onlinecounsellingcollege.tumblr.com/post/96727325003/the-secret-of-happiness" rel="bookmark" style="background: transparent; border: 0px; color: #111111; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline;"&gt;The Secret of Happiness&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/h1&gt;
&lt;/header&gt;&lt;section style="background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #111111; font-family: Georgia, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 22px;"&gt;&lt;div style="background: transparent; border: 0px; margin-bottom: 15px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;"&gt;
1.Recognize that happiness is a choice.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background: transparent; border: 0px; margin-bottom: 15px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;"&gt;
2. Forgive yourself for your past mistakes.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background: transparent; border: 0px; margin-bottom: 15px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;"&gt;
3. Stop being a victim of your circumstances.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background: transparent; border: 0px; margin-bottom: 15px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;"&gt;
4. Live each moment to the fullest.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background: transparent; border: 0px; margin-bottom: 15px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;"&gt;
5. Follow your heart, and do what you love.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background: transparent; border: 0px; margin-bottom: 15px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;"&gt;
6. Appreciate what you have; don&#8217;t fixate on what is missing.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background: transparent; border: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;"&gt;
7. Surround yourself with people you love.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/section&gt;
&lt;div style='clear: both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;

&lt;h2 class='date-header'&gt;
&lt;span&gt;
Sunday, 17 August 2014
&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;/h2&gt;

                                        &lt;div class="date-posts"&gt;
                                      
&lt;div class='post-outer'&gt;
&lt;div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'&gt;
&lt;meta content='2480335764212217316' itemprop='blogId'/&gt;
&lt;meta content='7780815858272769573' itemprop='postId'/&gt;
&lt;a name='7780815858272769573'&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
&lt;a href='http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/06/gratitude.html'&gt;
Gratitude
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7780815858272769573' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Gratitude is the quality of being thankful. As some unknown author said "The richest man is not he who has the most, but he who needs the least".&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Being grateful allow you to start making the most of what you have. This quality is important for Intellectual and emotional wellness. Intellectual wellness is how well you are able to use resources at your disposal to learn skills and expand knowledge which being grateful allows you to do more efficiently. Emotional wellness is how well you regulate your emotions along with the
 ability to understand ourselves and the ability to cope with life's 
challenges and being grateful allows you to see the good in every situation &lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
A Gratitude dairy is a good way to cultivate gratefulness. All is required is some method of recording and the discipline to record several things you are grateful for periodically. It could be as little as three things a week or as much as one hundred things a day&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Please leave a comment as to how much you found a gratitude diary helped.
&lt;div style='clear: both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;

&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
&lt;a href='http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/08/strength.html'&gt;
Strength
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8131955090305550306' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
&lt;div class="post_title large" style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-color: white; box-sizing: border-box; color: #343434; font-family: georgia, serif; font-size: 36px; line-height: 42px; margin-bottom: 10px; outline: none 0px;"&gt;
&#8220;&lt;span class="quote" style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box; outline: none 0px; text-rendering: optimizelegibility;"&gt;Out of your vulnerabilities will come your strength.&lt;/span&gt;&#8221;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="post_body" style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-color: white; box-sizing: border-box; color: #444444; float: left; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', HelveticaNeue, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; line-height: 19.600000381469727px; outline: none 0px; overflow: visible; padding-top: 2px; width: 500px;"&gt;
&lt;table class="quote_source_table" style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); border-collapse: collapse; border-width: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; outline: none 0px;"&gt;&lt;tbody style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box; outline: none 0px;"&gt;
&lt;tr style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); box-sizing: border-box; outline: none 0px;"&gt;&lt;td class="quote_source_mdash" style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); border-width: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; outline: none 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: text-top;"&gt;&#8212;&nbsp;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td class="quote_source" style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); border-width: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; outline: none 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: text-top;"&gt;Sigmund Freud&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;

&lt;h2 class='date-header'&gt;
&lt;span&gt;
Friday, 11 July 2014
&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;/h2&gt;

                                        &lt;div class="date-posts"&gt;
                                      
&lt;div class='post-outer'&gt;
&lt;div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'&gt;
&lt;meta content='2480335764212217316' itemprop='blogId'/&gt;
&lt;meta content='7086938961354241247' itemprop='postId'/&gt;
&lt;a name='7086938961354241247'&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
&lt;a href='http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/07/invictus.html'&gt;
Invictus
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7086938961354241247' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; padding-left: 1em; text-indent: -1em;"&gt;
Out of the night that covers me,&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; padding-left: 1em; text-indent: -1em;"&gt;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Black as the pit from pole to pole,&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; padding-left: 1em; text-indent: -1em;"&gt;
I thank whatever gods may be&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; padding-left: 1em; text-indent: -1em;"&gt;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;For my unconquerable soul.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px;" /&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; padding-left: 1em; text-indent: -1em;"&gt;
In the fell clutch of circumstance&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; padding-left: 1em; text-indent: -1em;"&gt;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;I have not winced nor cried aloud.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; padding-left: 1em; text-indent: -1em;"&gt;
Under the bludgeonings of chance&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; padding-left: 1em; text-indent: -1em;"&gt;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;My head is bloody, but unbowed.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px;" /&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; padding-left: 1em; text-indent: -1em;"&gt;
Beyond this place of wrath and tears&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; padding-left: 1em; text-indent: -1em;"&gt;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Looms but the Horror of the shade,&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; padding-left: 1em; text-indent: -1em;"&gt;
And yet the menace of the years&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; padding-left: 1em; text-indent: -1em;"&gt;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Finds and shall find me unafraid.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;br style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px;" /&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; padding-left: 1em; text-indent: -1em;"&gt;
It matters not how strait the gate,&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; padding-left: 1em; text-indent: -1em;"&gt;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;How charged with punishments the scroll,&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; padding-left: 1em; text-indent: -1em;"&gt;
I am the master of my fate,&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; padding-left: 1em; text-indent: -1em;"&gt;
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;I am the captain of my soul.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; padding-left: 1em; text-indent: -1em;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #505050; font-family: Georgia; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; padding-left: 1em; text-indent: -1em;"&gt;
&lt;a href="http://www.poetryfoundation.org/bio/william-ernest-henley" style="color: #043d6e; font-family: Arial; font-size: 12px; letter-spacing: 0.6000000238418579px; line-height: normal; outline: none; text-decoration: none; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: uppercase;"&gt;WILLIAM ERNEST HENLEY&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style='clear: both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;

&lt;a name='1930533290947176790'&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
&lt;a href='http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/07/ten-things-to-remember-and-one-thing-to.html'&gt;
Ten Things to Remember and One Thing to Never Forget
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-1930533290947176790' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
Your presence is a present to the world&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
You're truly one of a kind&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
Your life can be what you want it to be&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
Take the days one at a time&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
Count your blessings not your troubles&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
You'll make it through what ever comes along&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
Within you are some many answers&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
Have courage; be strong&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
Wish upon a star, and don't ever forget... How very special your are&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
by Collin McCarty&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style='clear: both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;

style="height: 168px; margin-left: -23px; margin-right: -39px; margin-top: 0px; width: 300px;" /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em; text-align: left;"&gt;
Sparx is an interactive game developed by researchers at Auckland University.Sparx was created by Dr Sally Merry, Dr Karolina Stasiask, Dr Theresa Fleming, Dr Matt Shepherd and Dr Mathijs Lucassen. Sparx won the World Summit Award in the category of e-Health and environment in 2011. It is designed as a e-therapy using cognitive behavioural therapy to help teenagers and adults deal with mild to moderate depression. In an experiment testing the effectiveness Sparx, about 43.7% &nbsp;of adolescents achieved remission in the SPARX group compared to the 26.4% in the usual care.&nbsp;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em; text-align: left;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em; text-align: left;"&gt;
Why don't you guys give it ago and leave a comment how you find it below!&lt;/div&gt;

&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4589986971569415708' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
&lt;a href="https://fbcdn-sphotos-h-a.akamaihd.net/hphotos-ak-xpf1/v/t34.0-12/10313420_327119834111890_8077989731317733157_n.jpg?oh=1b87ea2d1a0c413bcce252a12c1bcfe0&amp;oe=53BEF80B&amp;__gda__=1405019316_313f09e3b4d82d4cb81c7557b46225a1"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;img class="_4-od" data-reactid=".4m.0.0.1.1" src="https://fbcdn-sphotos-h-a.akamaihd.net/hphotos-ak-xpf1/v/t34.0-12/10313420_327119834111890_8077989731317733157_n.jpg?oh=1b87ea2d1a0c413bcce252a12c1bcfe0&amp;oe=53BEF80B&amp;__gda__=1405019316_313f09e3b4d82d4cb81c7557b46225a1" style="height: 727px; width: 625px;" /&gt;

                                        &lt;div class="date-outer"&gt;
                                      
&lt;h2 class='date-header'&gt;
&lt;span&gt;
Sunday, 6 July 2014
&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;/h2&gt;

                                        &lt;div class="date-posts"&gt;
                                      
&lt;div class='post-outer'&gt;
&lt;div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'&gt;
&lt;meta content='http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/Serotonin-2D-skeletal.svg/200px-Serotonin-2D-skeletal.svg.png' itemprop='image_url'/&gt;
&lt;meta content='2480335764212217316' itemprop='blogId'/&gt;
&lt;meta content='2663744681741542538' itemprop='postId'/&gt;
&lt;a name='2663744681741542538'&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
&lt;a href='http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/07/serotonin-happiness-neurotransmitter.html'&gt;
Serotonin - The Happiness Neurotransmitter
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2663744681741542538' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
&lt;b&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Serotonin&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;img alt="Skeletal formula of serotonin" data-file-height="214" data-file-width="304" src="http://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/Serotonin-2D-skeletal.svg/200px-Serotonin-2D-skeletal.svg.png" height="141" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/Serotonin-2D-skeletal.svg/300px-Serotonin-2D-skeletal.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/Serotonin-2D-skeletal.svg/400px-Serotonin-2D-skeletal.svg.png 2x" width="200" /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Serotonin is a monoamine neurotransmitter found in the gastrointestinal tract, platelets and the central nervous system of the body. While 90% of serotonin is found in the gastrointestinal tract, this post will focus on the role serotonin plays in the central nervous system.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;span style="color: #111111;"&gt;&lt;span style="background-color: #fdfdfd; line-height: 20.400001525878906px;"&gt;Serotonin is has some of the most diverse ac&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;span style="background-color: #fdfdfd; color: #111111; line-height: 20.400001525878906px;"&gt;tions of any physiological substance. Serotonin plays a role in&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;ul style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; background-color: #fdfdfd; border: 0px; color: #111111; line-height: 20.400001525878906px; list-style: square outside; margin: 20px 0px 30px 18px; padding: 0px 0px 0px 10px;"&gt;
&lt;li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; border: 0px; line-height: 1.35em; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;appetite&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; border: 0px; line-height: 1.35em; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;sleep&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; border: 0px; line-height: 1.35em; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;memory&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; border: 0px; line-height: 1.35em; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;learning&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; border: 0px; line-height: 1.35em; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;temperature&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; border: 0px; line-height: 1.35em; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;mood&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; border: 0px; line-height: 1.35em; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;behaviour&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; border: 0px; line-height: 1.35em; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;muscle contraction&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; border: 0px; line-height: 1.35em; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;depression&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; border: 0px; line-height: 1.35em; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;cardiovascular function&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; border: 0px; line-height: 1.35em; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;endocrine regulation&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; border: 0px; line-height: 1.35em; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;regulating aging&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; border: 0px; line-height: 1.35em; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;bone metabolism&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; border: 0px; line-height: 1.35em; margin: 0px 0px 10px; padding: 0px;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;wound healing&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;span style="color: #111111;"&gt;&lt;span style="line-height: 21.600000381469727px;"&gt;Serotonin&nbsp;is&nbsp;synthesised&nbsp;from tryptophan, an essential amino acid. Consuming tryptophan produces a calming effect in brain due to increased&nbsp;synthesis&nbsp;of&nbsp;serotonin.&nbsp;Tryptophan is found in&nbsp;bananas, pineapples, plums, turkeys and milk.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style='clear: both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-footer'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-footer-line post-footer-line-1'&gt;

&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
&lt;a href='http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/07/joshua-walters-on-being-just-crazy.html'&gt;
Joshua Walters - On Being Just Crazy Enough
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-1193280784432446101' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;object width="320" height="266" class="BLOGGER-youtube-video" classid="clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000" codebase="http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0" data-thumbnail-src="https://ytimg.googleusercontent.com/vi/ruvWiXowiZ8/0.jpg"&gt;&lt;param name="movie" value="https://youtube.googleapis.com/v/ruvWiXowiZ8&amp;source=uds" /&gt;&lt;param name="bgcolor" value="#FFFFFF" /&gt;&lt;param name="allowFullScreen" value="true" /&gt;&lt;embed width="320" height="266"  src="https://youtube.googleapis.com/v/ruvWiXowiZ8&amp;source=uds" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" allowfullscreen="true"&gt;&lt;/embed&gt;&lt;/object&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;span style="color: #333333; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px; line-height: 17px;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;span style="color: #333333; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px; line-height: 17px;"&gt;At TED's Full Spectrum Auditions, comedian Joshua Walters, who's bipolar, walks the line between mental illness and mental "skillness." In this funny, thought-provoking talk, he asks: What's the right balance between medicating craziness away and riding the manic edge of creativity and drive?&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;div style='clear: both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;

                                        &lt;div class="date-outer"&gt;
                                      
&lt;h2 class='date-header'&gt;
&lt;span&gt;
Friday, 4 July 2014
&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;/h2&gt;

                                        &lt;div class="date-posts"&gt;
                                      
&lt;div class='post-outer'&gt;
&lt;div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'&gt;
&lt;meta content='2480335764212217316' itemprop='blogId'/&gt;
&lt;meta content='480746342158457536' itemprop='postId'/&gt;
&lt;a name='480746342158457536'&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
&lt;a href='http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/07/8-ways-to-cope-when-you-feel-horrible.html'&gt;
 8 ways to cope when you feel horrible
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-480746342158457536' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
Some times when you have mental illness you feel horrible and there is nothing you can seem to do to feel better or get relief from negative experiences or emotions. The best option you have is to buckle down and ride out the negative emotions and try to put into practice as many of these tips as possible&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt;1. Acceptance&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
The best thing to do in this situation is to accept that you are not going to be able to function as well or feel as good as you used to. Acceptance does not meant that you approve of your situation, it means that you accept feeling horrible for what it is, and are willing to take the steps to manage your situation.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt;2. Reach out&nbsp;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
Talk to your friends and family and discuss the situation with them. When talking try to be solution focused, as just talking about how bad you are doing, may bring them and you down and is not productive.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt;3. &nbsp;Put off major life decisions and commitments for a while&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
Hopefully your situation is short term and not a chronic part of your life. In this case its important not to base any important decisions on how you feel at the moment. If it is possible try and put off some of the more energy consuming life commitments until you feel better.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt;4. Keep doing the basics&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
On the other hand it is important to keep doing the things you need to do to look after yourself and provide meaning in your life. Keep doing the basic things you need to do to survive and function. Feeling horrible is not a excuse for completely letting things slide.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt;5. Focus on what you can do&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
When acutely distressed it is hard to summon the motivation to do things you want to do or have to do. While distressed you might not be able to focus or concentrate. &nbsp;It pays to focus on the things that you can do and try to enjoy doing them.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt;6. Mindfulness&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
Mindfulness allows you to live and be concious in the present so you can avoid thinking about the suffering in the past and the future. Being mindful when things are tough is hard, but it allows you to experience the full range of human emotions which is important for a happy and healthy emotional life.&lt;br /&gt;
Read more about mindfulness &lt;a href="http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/06/mindfullness-101.html" target="_blank"&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; and &lt;a href="http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/06/mindfulness-102-how-to-be-mindful.html" target="_blank"&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/b&gt;
&lt;b&gt;7. H.A.L.T&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
Sometimes you may feel horrible due to low blood sugar, being dehydrated, feeling tired or having resentments. The H.A.L.T techniques takes care of the main fixable reasons of why you might feel horrible. Occasionally, all you need to do is have to time to yourself to refuel, sleep and talk to some loved ones to feel better. Read more about the H.A.L.T technique &lt;a href="http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/07/halt-technique.html" target="_blank"&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/b&gt;
&lt;b&gt;8. Practice gratitude&lt;/b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
Gratitude turns the negatives into your life into a positive. According to &lt;a href="http://greatergood.berkeley.edu/expandinggratitude" target="_blank"&gt;researchers&lt;/a&gt;&nbsp;practising gratitude regularly strengthens the immune system, provides higher levels of positive emotions, provides more joy, optimism and happiness and makes people feel less lonely and more connected. These benefits are great for someone who is feeling down and depressed. Read more &lt;a href="http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/06/grattitude-letter.html" target="_blank"&gt;here&lt;/a&gt; and &lt;a href="http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/06/gratitude.html" target="_blank"&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;.
&lt;div style='clear: both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;

&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
Hungry&lt;/div&gt;

gDIU6Z+ary4tQWZXBuWf48lTlnJUL3kpmqiVgViMKBitQhBMxisRsQxBWo28lAo2q9hXUyVdjFPG1QdJs3acrMnmltV0kO2pCLuJ8Vw+FeRY+a2sO63FBqzY4k5+RULsS79aqql4/BUb3jjmoDxE51FeizMRihwKmllHFZ00igCWYKjK8IsQ4KlK5UNIQq8iF71A56oT1C9J0lVA960MtOkjY1bUwCkYxEGgZnwR9/T7IosolZhzrbqi90c+uSrGSuZTbyC0Z/4aIXTKsZOHmgCYJXSE8kyAFFVASJqAKRqCWMK3Eq0ZVuAKC1EFbiKrRkK1G4LIk1ViByr7vAqVhKDRjIV2KWizIh5qxDXj0QaW+ELpFEx1NVBLLQ6UUDyk9VRnepppaZKlK+uYQVZHKrK5TTOCpyuVAPeq8jlJIq7iqAcVC4qRyieqKgICcyFRp1tT1TgoapIC3kqoU6gJOEIToCRBAnBQG1SNUTVI1RE7FbjKpNVuEqC3GVPGFWjViIVWRa3ealbbxVZTwoLcb6ZK3U0VaMK3GKoDEnoo3PGoQvFFBJnyKgKWYKjM/kpZb6qpMVRBK9VJCpZCFWkcrAD3KB6N5UBVAuKjcU7io3FUVkkklpSTpkkDp0ySBwU4TBJQEE6FEgMKRqiBRtUE7VYiVWMqwwoi2081YjVRgU8blmi2CjhkUFeCdiC+yaitQzkrNa5SByYL73EquXEKLvSge9QE96rSyVSleq0jqIBmVN7qKaR6gc9agjc9REp5FCXKh3FRkoi5RkoIUkklpSSSSQOEkkkDpJkkBBOhCIKAgjCjCMFBKxTsKrMKnaVEWmuUjHXVXeRscg0GHipmuVJj1I16gubyTZFXDkYdRBY7xBI5QF6F0iB3uUD3InPUL3oI3FQuKJ7lEXKgHqMhE4qMlADggqjchKqv/9k=" style="height: 186px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px; width: 232px;" /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="_A8 rg_ilm"&gt;
&lt;div class="rg_ilmbg"&gt;
&lt;span class="rg_ilmn"&gt; &nbsp; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
Tired&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;img class="rg_i" data-src="http://t0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcTVIJzJOlV9nue746bQgLpXtvOygkuWYJ24WIlGBVP5pwe1ptvGEg" data-sz="f" name="LG8Q_WC6lNvJ8M:" src="http://t0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcTVIJzJOlV9nue746bQgLpXtvOygkuWYJ24WIlGBVP5pwe1ptvGEg" style="height: 201px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: -6px; width: 250px;" /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="_A8 rg_ilm"&gt;
&lt;div class="rg_ilmbg"&gt;
&lt;span class="rg_ilmn"&gt;&nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="_A8 rg_ilm"&gt;
&lt;div class="rg_ilmbg" style="text-align: left;"&gt;
&lt;span class="rg_ilmn"&gt;Sometimes feeling a bit down or anxious can be traced back to low blood sugar levels from missing a meal or being dehydrated. You might be carrying some resentment, be a bit lonely or &lt;/span&gt;just be plain tired.&lt;span class="rg_ilmn"&gt; All you have to do is to check in with yourself how you are feeling in that moment every hour or so. If you feel any of these feelings , then take the appropriate steps to get your needs met. H.A.L.T can stand for a lot of things such as Hygiene, Anxiety, Lazy, Thirsty. The H.A.L.T technique is a great tool for managing your moods and getting more in touch with how you are feeling.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="rg_ilmbg" style="text-align: left;"&gt;
&lt;span class="rg_ilmn"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="rg_ilmbg" style="text-align: left;"&gt;
&lt;span class="rg_ilmn"&gt;A challenge to you is to employ the H.A.L.T technique for three days and see if it makes any difference for you.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style='clear: both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;

&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
&lt;a href='http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/07/free-writing.html'&gt;
Free Writing
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8768394285159168042' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;div style="background-color: white; color: #353535; line-height: 35px; margin: 40px 0px 10px; text-rendering: optimizelegibility;"&gt;
&lt;span style="font-size: small;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;There are as many benefits of writing as there are ways to write. Stream of consciousness writing (aka Free writing) is a good way to unload your worries and to express yourself. The only rules of free writing is that you just write what comes into your head without editing for a certain amount of time. There doesn't need to be any format, grammar or sentence structure. The benefits of free writing include &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: small;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;There are no expectations, you don't have to write a great piece of literature so there is no pressure or performance anxiety&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: small;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;You can easily produce a lot of good material in a short amount of time&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;span style="font-size: small;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: small;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;Stream of consciousness writing is great for producing new ideas or revelations&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;span style="font-size: small;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: small;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;You can express yourself and learn about how you think&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt; &lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;span style="font-size: small;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;span style="font-size: small;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
&lt;span style="font-size: small;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: inherit;"&gt;The best way to learn how to write is to do a bit everyday. Read about how to form a habit &lt;a href="http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/06/how-to-form-habit.html" target="_blank"&gt;here&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style='clear: both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-footer'&gt;

&lt;a href='http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/07/jon-ronson-strange-answers-to.html'&gt;
Jon Ronson - Strange answers to the psychopath test
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-2854342843490113051' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;
&lt;object width="320" height="266" class="BLOGGER-youtube-video" classid="clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000" codebase="http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0" data-thumbnail-src="https://ytimg.googleusercontent.com/vi/xYemnKEKx0c/0.jpg"&gt;&lt;param name="movie" value="https://youtube.googleapis.com/v/xYemnKEKx0c&amp;source=uds" /&gt;&lt;param name="bgcolor" value="#FFFFFF" /&gt;&lt;param name="allowFullScreen" value="true" /&gt;&lt;embed width="320" height="266"  src="https://youtube.googleapis.com/v/xYemnKEKx0c&amp;source=uds" type="application/x-shockwave-flash" allowfullscreen="true"&gt;&lt;/embed&gt;&lt;/object&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
Is there a definitive line that divides crazy from sane? With a 
hair-raising delivery, Jon Ronson, author of The Psychopath Test, 
illuminates the gray areas between the two.
&lt;div style='clear: both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
