&lt;a name='7424154503427507091'&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'&gt;
&lt;a href='http://significantsentience.blogspot.co.nz/2014/06/improving-wellness.html'&gt;
Improving Wellness
&lt;/a&gt;
&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header'&gt;
&lt;div class='post-header-line-1'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7424154503427507091' itemprop='articleBody'&gt;
Wellness may seem life a far off concept when in the grips of mental illness. Wellness is about making choices. People already make a lot of choices in their lives that they have control over. A basic example is what to eat and when to eat it. So why not make the choices you have positive ones? Wellness is getting actively involved in your life and working to make choices to improve every aspect of life.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;div class="_YA"&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="_YA"&gt;
Wellness
 is an active process of becoming aware of and making choices toward a 
healthy and fulfilling life. "...a state of complete physical, mental, 
and social well-being, and not merely the absence of disease or 
infirmity." - The World Health Organization.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
There are seven basic types of wellness which will be covered below&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Physical wellness is exercising to keep fit, eating right to meet nutritional needs, getting adequate length and quality of sleep and generally looking after your body. An example of increasing physical wellness would be deciding to drink more water or deciding to walk more. Improving physical fitness is important to give you the energy and longevity to get through life. &lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Social wellness is how connected you are with your friends, family and society. A simple way to learn to be more social is to challenge your self to talk to a new person or an old friend everyday. Social wellness is important as we humans are social beings. Our ability to co-operate has given rise to many marvels. Social skills are important to foster connections between people&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Emotional wellness is how well you regulate your emotions along with the ability to understand ourselves and the ability to cope with life's challenges. Emotional wellness is important to our ability to function in the world. One way to increase emotional wellness is learning the skill of mindfulness. (There will be a post soon about this)&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Spiritual wellness is the ability for someone to identify and act accordingly with their values. This is important to reduce the amount of distress that is caused by acting against our morals. One way of improving spiritual wellness is to write out a list of values and rank them in order of importance to you.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Environmental wellness is how well someone understands what impact you have on your surroundings and the efforts taken to make a reduce negative effects and increase positive effects. Environmental wellness is important because so far we only have one habitable planet. A way to increase environmental wellness is to recycle&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Intellectual wellness is how well you are able to use resources at your disposal to learn skills and expand knowledge. Intellectual wellness is important for active participation in scholastic, cultural, and community activities. A fun way to increase intellectual wellness is to visit &lt;a href="http://www.wikihow.com/Main-Page" target="_blank"&gt; Wikihow&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
Time management&lt;b&gt; &lt;/b&gt;is consciously choosing how you spend time on activates. Time management is important as it increases effectiveness, efficiency and productivity. A good way to help with time management is to plan each day in half hour blocks the day before.&lt;br /&gt;
&lt;div class="_YA"&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="_YA"&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;
A good challenge is to try and think of one or more ways to improve each area of wellness and take a small step toward achieving it.&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="_YA"&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div class="_YA"&gt;
Please feel free to leave a comment and discuss below about how you are going to improve your wellness!&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;div style='clear: both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
